  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_5027b40b-00c8-46d9-b8dc-b224c841dd28'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

<span id="freeTextContainer15374629958950446810">Alayna Withers relationship with Hudson Pierce has tested both her and his ability to trust. They decide that the only way they can move forward together is with open doors and transparency. It won’t be easy for the scarred lovers, but they’re committed to each other more now than ever. Alayna, in particular, has grown through their trials, and has emerged more confident a</span>
  <span id="freeText15374629958950446810" style="display:none">Alayna Withers relationship with Hudson Pierce has tested both her and his ability to trust. They decide that the only way they can move forward together is with open doors and transparency. It won’t be easy for the scarred lovers, but they’re committed to each other more now than ever. Alayna, in particular, has grown through their trials, and has emerged more confident and faithful to the man she loves. <br /><br />But while the pair is focused on the future, their past shows up again to threaten their fragile bond. Promises that were made are broken, and Alayna learns that Hudson still has very potent secrets—secrets that will tear them both apart. As much as she feels for him, her ability to forgive and forget is tested beyond her limits. <br /><br />Even though she found the only man who could fix her, a forever with Hudson seems more and more out of reach.</span>

<div id="bookReviews">
  




  <div class="friendReviews elementListBrown" >
    <div class="section firstReview">
      

<div id="review_681645145" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/681645145" />
    <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog"><img alt="Aestas Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353371225p2/5604583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/681645145?book_show_action=true">Jul 30, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>
      </span>

          added it




        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer681645145" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10207135752975776235"><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389657022i/8046045._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>First, here's my casting....<br/><img width='100%' src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380431188ra/865102.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>**** FULL REVIEW NOW POSTED ****<br/><br/><b> Hudson Pierce is back!!!!! </b><br/><br/>Please note that this book is the third and final instalment in The Fixed Trilogy and is not intended to be read as a standalone as it is a direct continuation of the story from the previous books.<br/><br/>This one picks up right where the last book ended with that one burning question that we were left with and my heart was in knots while wondering how that secret could potentially come between them.<br/><br/>Despite their res</span>
  <span id="freeText10207135752975776235" style="display:none"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389657022i/8046045._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>First, here's my casting....<br><img width="100%" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380431188ra/865102.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>**** FULL REVIEW NOW POSTED ****<br><br><b> Hudson Pierce is back!!!!! </b><br><br>Please note that this book is the third and final instalment in The Fixed Trilogy and is not intended to be read as a standalone as it is a direct continuation of the story from the previous books.<br><br>This one picks up right where the last book ended with that one burning question that we were left with and my heart was in knots while wondering how that secret could potentially come between them.<br><br>Despite their respective issues though, Hudson and Alayna loved each other very deeply. Even though mistakes had been made and trust had been broken in the past, the one thing that held strong how much they both so clearly wanted to make this relationship work.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"I knew our love outweighed the heaviness of those mistakes."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>What I loved about them was that they both were quite .... well, "damaged" isn't really the right word per se, but they were both struggling with certain compulsions that their pasts had almost turned into habit. But they both understood where their issues lay and they were both willing to work at changing themselves and helping each other take steps towards being more healthy both individually and as a couple.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"We both have to change. We have to put everything out on the line, Hudson, as much as possible. We know now that we're together, thick and thin, right? We have to trust that more than anything. We can't be afraid of our secrets and our pasts. Both of us. Honesty, open doors, transparency."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>What I loved was that we got to see several scenarios created by the direction of the plot which <em>could</em> have led to more mistakes being made on both their parts but I was so thrilled to see them taking the right path and making the right choices instead of repeating the mistakes of their past. It clearly showed that they had both grown a lot over the course of their relationship.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"We have the future to make up for the hurts we've cause each other."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>As with the first two books, the character dynamic here were great! I loved the writing too -- it continued in the same, strong, compelling style that I'd come to love in this series. I also loved the interjections of humor now and again too that helped lighten the mood even if it was sometimes at Hudson's expense ;)<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"Jealousy doesn't look good on you, son."</em>
    <br>
    <em> I disagreed. Jealousy did look good on Hudson. Quite good indeed.</em>
    <br>
    <em> A low grumble came from the back of his throat.</em>
    <br>
    <em> Jack cocked his head. "Did he just growl?"</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>It brought a smile to my face watching Hudson and Alayna work through their issues and make concessions for each other along the way. They both had a strong understanding of each other's fears and genuinely tried to help make things better. With the way it was portrayed, it almost made it relatable because it was written in such a way that really made you genuinely understand their mind set.<br><br>Now, the entire story is told from Alayna's POV which was wonderful in some respects because it <em>really</em> made her a very relatable heroine as it was so easy to understand what drove her insecurities and what she was feeling. But seeing only one side of the story also made everything regarding Hudson a huge mystery.<br><br>He loved her. There was <em>no</em> doubt about that. I mean, his words speak for themselves...<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"You're the center of my world precious. Every minute of every day. Even when I'm not with you."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>...but he was hiding something big -- a devastating secret that genuinely had the power to tear them apart.<br><br>I'm not going to deny that at this point, I got <em>very</em> frustrated with Hudson. It was actually an interesting situation because in most books I find myself frustrated with the heroine for one reason or another and in this book, it was the hero who I wanted to shake. I was fully Team Alayna at this point because he shut down and refused to talk about anything despite their promises of openness. And this closed-off attitude put an understandably huge wall between them.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"I have no answers to give you. This subject is closed."<br>"Are you kidding me? You're not going to talk about this?"<br>"No, I'm not."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br><br>OMG I was going <em>nuts</em> trying to figure out what his angle was. What was he up to?? I was right there in the same boat as Laynie -- I <em>wanted</em> to trust him, but his actions and secrets made it <em>so fucking hard</em>. I guess I really have to tip my hat to the author here for putting my <em>right</em> in the heroine's mind and having me experience the exact same things as her because dammit, I was reaching the limits of my patience and understanding with him. He literally pushed me to the very brink and almost over. I was angry with him. Furious. There didn't seem to be any justifications for his actions and he was literally forcing Laynie to deal with her worst nightmare. How could he not see that???<br><br>But here's the interesting thing -- I was more frustrated with this part of the story <em>while</em> I was reading than I was afterward. Because looking back on it now and <em>knowing</em> what his secret was, I kinda get it. I still think he was wrong to keep it from her and there was no doubt that that was a huge mistake on his part but... nobody's perfect and we all knew the demons he was fighting. And honestly -- his secret <em>was</em> bad enough that once I found out what it was, I did at least understand <em>why </em>he would have wanted to hide it.<br><br>While the back and forth in this part of the story did frustrate me a little, I also recognize that working through issues is a part of what makes a relationship stronger. I felt like especially given their particular set of problems and weaknesses, this was the kind of hurdle that would make or break their relationship and there was no doubt in my mind that if they could face <em>this</em> and come out on top, that they could face anything.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"I don't have all the answers yet. But we can work on it together. We fix each other, remember?"</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>At it's core, this was a story of two deeply damaged people who loved each other deeply fighting a lifetime of compulsions and making up for potentially unforgivable mistakes. But the fact that, even in their worst moment, they still loved each other was was what got me through the harder parts of this book.<br><br>And when it was good between them.... just WOW. My heart soared. It was beautiful. I don't want to spoil anything but there some scenes that had me gasping out loud in happiness!! Not to mention that I do love me a good grovel and there was a healthy dose of grovelling here ;)<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"Even though I don't deserve it, I'm determined to fight to earn back your trust. Even if it takes the rest of my life."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>I won't spoil the ending but I will say that I loved it and that we're treated to a beautiful epilogue from Hudson's POV that just made all the hardship they went through worth it and brought their story full circle. It was heartwarming and just a perfect, very fitting end to the series.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"We know that we're worth the fight. SHE'S worth the fight…. She's mine. And I'm hers. Completely and absolutely."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br><br>The Fixed series delivers a scorching hot romance, heart stopping emotion, and a plot that will keep you glued to the page. Once I started reading, I could not put it down. This really was a wonderful trilogy!! I loved it and would highly recommend it especially for fans of Crossfire who are looking for something new to try that is unique in it's story but similar in it's vibe. If you loved Gideon Cross, then you have to meet Hudson Pierce!<br><br><strong>Rating: 4.5 stars</strong><br><br>Here's my Hudson casting.... (also see above)<br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431188i/865103._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Here are my other 2 reviews in the series: <br>#1 - <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/678271011">http://www.goodreads.com/review/show/...</a><br>#2 - <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/681640276">http://www.goodreads.com/review/show/...</a><br><br>****************************<br><br><b> For more of my reviews, book news and updates:<br>✦ <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Main blog: Aestas Book Blog</a><br>✦ <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook Blog Page</a><br>✦ <a href="https://twitter.com/AestasBookBlog" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> <br><br><a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380306821i/688100._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a></b></span>

<div id="review_787230728" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/787230728" />
    <a title="Debra" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13247178-debra"><img alt="Debra" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1473718933p2/13247178.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/787230728?book_show_action=true">Dec 11, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Debra" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Debra" href="/user/show/13247178-debra">Debra</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=swoonworthy-male-lead">swoonworthy-male-lead</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=2014-release">2014-release</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer787230728" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14419573826747735597"><br/>★★★★ <b>4 'Fixed' stars!</b><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>"Without struggle there is no progress."</i>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390069367i/8138290.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Forever With You</b> is the third and final part of the Fixed-series by Laurelin Paige and it picks up right where the previous part ended. Since I really liked the previous two books in the series, I was very much looking forward to find out how Hudson and Alayna's story would end. Throughout the story, Alayna's jealousy and insecurity did annoy me at times, though I did understand where she was coming from. And Hudson has become even</span>
  <span id="freeText14419573826747735597" style="display:none"><br>★★★★ <b>4 'Fixed' stars!</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>"Without struggle there is no progress."</i>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390069367i/8138290.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Forever With You</b> is the third and final part of the Fixed-series by Laurelin Paige and it picks up right where the previous part ended. Since I really liked the previous two books in the series, I was very much looking forward to find out how Hudson and Alayna's story would end. Throughout the story, Alayna's jealousy and insecurity did annoy me at times, though I did understand where she was coming from. And Hudson has become even more swoon worthy now that he's finally admitting his true feelings toward Alayna, even though it takes him quite a while to get there.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"You're the first person I've ever loved, Alayna. And I know you'll be the last."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390069367i/8138291.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Alayna Withers</b> has always had trouble connecting with people. Her commitment issues were of the kind that she always got <i>too</i> attached to the men in her life and even went as far as too stalk them and follow them around when they didn't return her affections. But now that she's finally overcome her stalker tendencies, she's been able to build up a seemingly healthy and stable relationship with Hudson, who never judged her because of her past.<br><br>Still, the fact that Hudson believed Celia over her for a short period of time hurt her more than she could have imagined. It has made her self esteem fragile and she's become even more insecure than before. Then, there's the fact that Celia keeps coming back into her and Hudson's life which makes it all the more difficult for her to get past her trust issues. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>"You belong to me, precious. You belong with me. I won't let anything come between us. I won't let anything hurt you."</i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390069367i/8138292.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Hudson Pierce</b> has never really let anyone get too close to him. From the moment he realized how many women were attracted to him and how easily it was for him to manipulate them with his charm, he's made it his sport to play women by making them fall for him and then leave them heartbroken behind. But Alayna has always been different. She's the only one who's been able to brake through his exterior and find a way into his heart. Still, he hasn't told her all of his darkest secrets and he's afraid that when he does, she'll never be able to forgive him. So, he tries to deflect and avoid her many questions. But in the end it's proven once again that keeping secrets never turns out so great...<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Here I am, precious. I give myself freely. All of me, Alayna. No more walls or secrets or games or lies. I give you all of me, honestly. For forever, if you'll take it."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Overall, I really enjoyed reading this series. It was original, with just the right amount of drama and the perfect combination of romance and passion. I was happy with the way the story ended even though I would have liked the epilogue to be a little longer but that's just a minor detail. All in all, Forever With You was the perfect conclusion to Hudson and Laynie's story and I'm already looking forward to Gwen's story in the spin-off of this series.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390069367i/8138293.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <i><b>"Where is the road to your heart?"</b> With one finger, he lifted my chin to meet his eyes.<br><b>"Don't you know? You're the one who paved it."</b></i>
</blockquote><br><br></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Katy Loves Romance ❤️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Katy Loves Romance ❤️" href="/user/show/10247668-katy-loves-romance">Katy Loves Romance ❤️</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10247668-katy-loves-romance?shelf=conquer-my-tbr-in-2015">conquer-my-tbr-in-2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10247668-katy-loves-romance?shelf=conquer-my-tbr-shelf-in-2016">conquer-my-tbr-shelf-in-2016</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1150204906" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5978942891612493264"><b>4.75 Beautiful overall Fixed Stars</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/book%20collages/2DBA5C1D-CBA5-4FD4-957F-A3252146B3AF_zps5q48fbmj.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1452984541i/17769728._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo 2DBA5C1D-CBA5-4FD4-957F-A3252146B3AF_zps5q48fbmj.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>This is one of those series that was sitting on my TBR list forever, I had them on my kindle yet picked up other more new releases than this one. But hey here I am going back wanting to catch up on old series, so why not right?? <br/><br/>I have to say that initially it didn't grab me in full force that I usually like, I love Hudson and his dominant personality and magnitude, and likewise Alayna and her kickass strength that I loved. But this series has a very importa</span>
  <span id="freeText5978942891612493264" style="display:none"><b>4.75 Beautiful overall Fixed Stars</b><br><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/book%20collages/2DBA5C1D-CBA5-4FD4-957F-A3252146B3AF_zps5q48fbmj.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1452984541i/17769728._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 2DBA5C1D-CBA5-4FD4-957F-A3252146B3AF_zps5q48fbmj.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This is one of those series that was sitting on my TBR list forever, I had them on my kindle yet picked up other more new releases than this one. But hey here I am going back wanting to catch up on old series, so why not right?? <br><br>I have to say that initially it didn't grab me in full force that I usually like, I love Hudson and his dominant personality and magnitude, and likewise Alayna and her kickass strength that I loved. But this series has a very important plot that bit by bit unraveled as I read it, as I started to see into the secret, lies and characters that I enjoyed to hate and detest!!! I was seeing why certain people were important to how things were mapped out, why hudsons mum acted the way she is, who Hudsons father is?? Hudson's sister Mia and Celia well if I <b>EVER</b> hated a character then it has to be her... I loved everything about learning the importance of their roles, and to me this was like a puzzle that I was trying to put together before it happened. If you've read it you'll understand what I'm trying to say here. <br><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/book%20collages/F717077F-E376-42D5-9BC8-16F397E8A1BE_zps6kxty7sm.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1452984541i/17769729._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo F717077F-E376-42D5-9BC8-16F397E8A1BE_zps6kxty7sm.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Sensual, intriguing... Beautiful intrquiete plot... Sexy, magnetic characters that had me holding on for dear life.. I have met my new BFF broken heroes having me grabbing ahold of the words I want to savour them, hold them and help them... <br><br>Alayna is vulnerable because of her addiction, which are the kind of qualities I love. She's sassy and Fiesty and strong because of how she lives and how she deals with the hand she's been given. But I adore the way she handles herself likewise. <br><br><b>***Overall this was a slow developed story that gripped hold on my bones and tangled itself into my day, I'll now feel very lost without these characters but so help me God have I loved being alongside their journey...</b><br><br>Looking forward to reading Gwens books at some point. <br> </span>

<div id="review_818880074" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/818880074" />
    <a title="Angie - Angie&#39;s Dreamy Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8524618-angie---angie-s-dreamy-reads"><img alt="Angie - Angie&#39;s Dreamy Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1578074503p2/8524618.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/818880074?book_show_action=true">Jan 09, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Angie - Angie&#39;s Dreamy Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Angie - Angie&#39;s Dreamy Reads" href="/user/show/8524618-angie---angie-s-dreamy-reads">Angie - Angie&#39;s Dreamy Reads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer818880074" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3190342068460616674">Hudson Pierce <b>
  <i>**fans self**</i>
</b> God!!! I'm actually teary writing this review and I feel sad. It's a mix between a series hangover and depression.<br/><br/>Is this really our last Huds book? I can't believe it!!!!! I don't want to believe it :(<br/><br/>First and foremost, this book was the <b>PERFECT</b> ending to the series!!!!! Honestly third books are tough. The sex is always a little heavy, the plot can get boring, it can be overly sappy - almost losing the angst that the first two in the series had. It's really hard</span>
  <span id="freeText3190342068460616674" style="display:none">Hudson Pierce <b>
  <i>**fans self**</i>
</b> God!!! I'm actually teary writing this review and I feel sad. It's a mix between a series hangover and depression.<br /><br />Is this really our last Huds book? I can't believe it!!!!! I don't want to believe it :(<br /><br />First and foremost, this book was the <b>PERFECT</b> ending to the series!!!!! Honestly third books are tough. The sex is always a little heavy, the plot can get boring, it can be overly sappy - almost losing the angst that the first two in the series had. It's really hard. But I'd say Forever with You was not. The author kept our hearts pumping and <b>HOLY SHIT!</b> She breaks us....I'm was on the floor crying,<i>"What!!! How could you? ...omg :/ How? Why? Why? What the hell? Hudson...oh Alayna.... *sobs*</i><br /><br />Definitely angst!!!<br /><br />We get a huge <b>SECRET</b> in this book. Something <b>YOU WOULD NEVER SEE COMING.</b> Or at least I didn't. I'm terrible at figuring things out, so it hit me like a bulldozer. Celia is back *arg* and Stacy's video is brought up, of course. Remember the end of book two? Welp...Ha! <b>ANGST!</b> Seriously, Hud's and Alayna have a lot to work through. Not only getting past what happened at the end of book two when Hud's didn't believe her, but the feeling of betrayal that she carries with her. <br /><br />It's a push and pull of whether Alayna should trust this man she loves, who says he's transparent, but really isn't. Hudson is hiding something and refuses to open up to her. He's always asking her to trust him. But, trust is earned and this book is <b>ALL</b> based on this couple building that trust! <br /><br />You know really I love Alayna. I really do. I "get her." Yes, she's crazy jealous, but I can really <b>RELATE</b> to that. Haven't you ever sneaked or probed on your hubs or boyfriend? *winces, while averting eyes* I can say I have definitely snooped a time or two. <br /><br />She's just relatable. <br /><br />I always feel what she feels! I get jealous with her , turned on with her, angry with her, hurt with her, broken with her and crazy with her. I felt like I became her in this series. Even though she's a little crazy, she was <b>EVERY</b> girl that wants to matter and be loved. She's seeking validation. She goes a little over board, <b>BUT</b> in the final installment she <b>BLOOMS.</b> Talk about growing up. God, I honestly love the girl. I have to say she may be my favorite female fictional character. I just feel like I get her. <br /><br />Hudson, boy oh boy. Hud's, he's .....he's something in this one alright. I was fucking stunned while reading. I'm not going to lie!!! I might have wanted to kick the shit out of him. Maybe even maim him at one point. But oh my God, I love freaking the man. Like <b>FULL ON LOVE HIM!</b> He grows up too! He's deliciously dominant, but so sweet and marshmallowy on the inside..<b>INCREDIBLE.</b> <br /><br />He'll forever and ever be in my top five <b>BEST BOOK BOYFRIENDS EVER!</b> <br /><br />Hud's and Alayna's story grows. We may think we know Hudson Pierce but we don't!!! The plot sizzles in the final book and the punches that are thrown are epic. <br /><br />Overall this is a <b>FIVE</b> star series for me. I love them both and I'm sad it's done!!!!!!! <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="3190342068460616674" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer6633116789692414270">Accelerating tension and angst<br/>Big ugly secret.(Remember "Cruel Intentions"?)<br/>Bigger love than the big ugly secret.<br/>Right amount of groveling.<br/>Excellent ending.<br/><br/><b>
  <i>“Not only does my world revolve around her, but she is my world. She's not just my reason for breathing, she's air itself. She's the meaning behind every one of my thoughts, every thrum of my pulse, every whisper of my conscience. She's my entire everything. It's as simple and as complex as that.” </i>
</b><br/><br/>One of my favourite series of all time th</span>
  <span id="freeText6633116789692414270" style="display:none">Accelerating tension and angst<br />Big ugly secret.(Remember "Cruel Intentions"?)<br />Bigger love than the big ugly secret.<br />Right amount of groveling.<br />Excellent ending.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“Not only does my world revolve around her, but she is my world. She's not just my reason for breathing, she's air itself. She's the meaning behind every one of my thoughts, every thrum of my pulse, every whisper of my conscience. She's my entire everything. It's as simple and as complex as that.” </i>
</b><br /><br />One of my favourite series of all time that involves alpha billionaires, possessive and obsessive stalkers and true love! <br />(Although I am still not sure if I like Hudson...)</span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/690759471?book_show_action=true">Aug 09, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" href="/user/show/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog">Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=guy-is-a-douchebag-but-i-love-him">guy-is-a-douchebag-but-i-love-him</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer690759471" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer11214949195807950182">4 In Love With Hudson Stars<br/>(BR w/Melissa)<br/><br/><a href='http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/image_zps36cf2090.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390107762i/8145155._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo image_zps36cf2090.jpg' width='400' height='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><br/>Forever With You is the third and final installment to the story of Hudson and Laynie.<br/>We pick up at about where we left off from the last book.<br/>Hudson and Laynie are back together, but still on shaky ground.<br/>Laynie is still very much hurting over the fact that Hudson believed Celia's lies over Laynie's truths!!<br/>In the beginning of the story, I really couldn't stand Laynie.<br/>Even though Hudson apologized to her and the truth of Celia's deceptions were out, </span>
  <span id="freeText11214949195807950182" style="display:none">4 In Love With Hudson Stars<br>(BR w/Melissa)<br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/image_zps36cf2090.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390107762i/8145155._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo image_zps36cf2090.jpg" width="400" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>Forever With You is the third and final installment to the story of Hudson and Laynie.<br>We pick up at about where we left off from the last book.<br>Hudson and Laynie are back together, but still on shaky ground.<br>Laynie is still very much hurting over the fact that Hudson believed Celia's lies over Laynie's truths!!<br>In the beginning of the story, I really couldn't stand Laynie.<br>Even though Hudson apologized to her and the truth of Celia's deceptions were out, she still had moments where she was a blubbering idiot.<br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/5701020_zpse443533e.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1390107762ra/8145156.gif" alt=" photo 5701020_zpse443533e.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>Bitch Celia is still present in this one.<br>I was hoping the bitch would take a flying leap off the Empire State Building!!!<br>She was just constantly following Laynie around, and I knew the bitch still had something up her sleeve.<br><br>I found Hudson to be the PERFECT Book Boyfriend!<br>He was so attentive to Laynie in every way and I just thought it was weird that he loved when she would have her super jealous and possessive episodes over him.<br>He claimed that it made him feel loved, but it just gave me an uneasy feeling.<br>Hudson admitted that he would pretend to be into women in the past just for fun.<br>He was the master manipulator.<br>I thought of the movie "Cruel Intentions".<br>This had to be what was going on.<br>Hudson was pretending to be in love with Laynie.<br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/cruel-intentions-enemies-enemy-gif-kathryn-merteuil-Favimcom-290425_zpsa6375c94.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1390107762ra/8145157.gif" alt=" photo cruel-intentions-enemies-enemy-gif-kathryn-merteuil-Favimcom-290425_zpsa6375c94.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/image_zps98e766aa.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390107762i/8145158._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo image_zps98e766aa.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br><br>Hudson is hiding stuff from Laynie.<br>He's making late night calls to one of his female employees and having business meetings with her outside of work.<br>This sets off Laynie's old insecurities and she starts acting like the crazy jealous girlfriend with stalkerish tendencies.<br><br><br>At this point I'm still really not liking Laynie, but loving Hudson.<br><br>Until....she finally confronts Celia, and punches the bitch in the face!!! YEAH!!!!!<br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/tumblr_m4je0vtavO1rrgulmo1_500_zps30a60c96.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1390107762ra/8145159.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_m4je0vtavO1rrgulmo1_500_zps30a60c96.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>Unfortunately, truths are revealed and I was only partially right about what I thought was going on.<br>I felt really bad for Laynie.<br>She was so utterly devastated.<br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/original_zpsf5662967.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1390107762ra/8145160.gif" alt=" photo original_zpsf5662967.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>I have to say that eventually Laynie pulls herself together and she had truly grown.<br>She didn't fall back into her old habits.<br>She was stronger.<br>I admired her strength in the end.<br><br><br>I knew Hudson had to go through hell to win her back.<br>I loved how he handled Celia!! <br>The bitch gets it back ten fold!!! <br>That's right, Celia, Karma's a BITCH!!!<br>He really turned out to be such an incredible Swoonworthy book boyfriend and he is the main reason why I rated this series highly.<br>Without him, I'd have given this a three.<br>My only complaint about Hudson, was his term of endearment, "precious".<br>How is that sexy??!<br>I kept picturing, Gollum, from "The Lord of the Rings"!!<br><br><br>Overall, this was an enjoyable read and I loved the Epilogue!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="11214949195807950182" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/685445057" />
    <a title="Jamie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11971939-jamie"><img alt="Jamie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1450934094p2/11971939.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/685445057?book_show_action=true">Aug 03, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jamie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jamie" href="/user/show/11971939-jamie">Jamie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11971939-jamie?shelf=couldnt-put-down">couldnt-put-down</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11971939-jamie?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11971939-jamie?shelf=all-time-fav">all-time-fav</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11971939-jamie?shelf=possessive">possessive</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11971939-jamie?shelf=twist">twist</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer685445057" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15315667947616683542"><i>
  <b> Hudson Pierce.... 5 dreamy stars... </b>
</i><br/><br/><br/>What a FANTISTIC ending to this series! I've loved each book, but I think this one was the best.... I loved Hudson just as much in this one as the others and I ended up liking Alayna even more this time. I know many got tired of her whining and jealousy throughout this series.. but that's just who she is.. she's been a work in progress and has seriously come a long way. Most of the issues with Hudson and Alayna in this installment, I feel, lay squarely on</span>
  <span id="freeText15315667947616683542" style="display:none"><i>
  <b> Hudson Pierce.... 5 dreamy stars... </b>
</i><br /><br /><br />What a FANTISTIC ending to this series! I've loved each book, but I think this one was the best.... I loved Hudson just as much in this one as the others and I ended up liking Alayna even more this time. I know many got tired of her whining and jealousy throughout this series.. but that's just who she is.. she's been a work in progress and has seriously come a long way. Most of the issues with Hudson and Alayna in this installment, I feel, lay squarely on the shoulders of Hudson Pierce.. As much as I love that man, I seriously wanted to kick his ass.. especially when a MAJOR SECRET was revealed !! One that I totally did not see coming! And the more I think about this secret.. it really doesn't make a whole lot of sense for what happened in book 2 to even have been able to happen... spoiler below<br /><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ in book 2, shitty ass Celia played Alayna and set her up to seem like she was stalking and harassing Celia.. when it all came to a head, although Hudson defended Alayna, he still believed what Celia was saying.. so in book 3, we find out that to begin with, Alayna was a mark in a game that H and Celia used to play. Hudson didn't want to play because he fell for Alayna... SO, IF HUDSON KNEW WHAT A TOTAL SHIT CELIA WAS AND THAT SHE WAS LIKLEY STILL PLAYING THE GAME, HOW COULD HE HAVE EVEN FOR A SECOND BELEIVED ANYTHING THAT CELIA WAS SAYING ABOUT WHAT ALAYNA WAS DOING??  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />OK, so that one thing does not really make sense, but I can over look it since the rest of the story was so good and I loved having a little extra angst and drama thrown in.. but still--- I do think that part of the story could have been done differently to make more sense. <br /><br /><br />But in the end, fantastic series!</span>
  <a data-text-id="15315667947616683542" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer13380928768021043679">FIRST OF ALL.. LETS STARE AT THE COVER FOR A MINUTE AND ADMIRE IT.<br/>This series has the hottest covers.. **swoon!!**<br/><br/>Secondly, I'd like to thank the author.<br/>Thank you Laurelin for not fucking the book up!! :D<br/>Very rarely do you get to see the last book of a series which is actually good and lives up to people's expectations.<br/>I'm so glad this book lived up :D<br/><br/>I truly enjoyed reading this book, it was wonderful.<br/><br/>Hudson is just *sigh* <br/>Alayna is so strong and beautiful.<br/></span>

          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/20420468-forever-with-you">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer680803770" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6033717357533413554"><br/><br/>5++++ Stars<br/><br/>Another Trilogy I am sad to see end! Another couple that have cemented themselves as favorites of mine. I love a book that you cannot put down, I was trying to read every chance I get, at work, when I stopped at the traffic lights and definitely did not sleep that night trying to finish it! Yup I was it's bitch!!!<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389698327ra/8049029.gif' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/>It was amazing, certainly outdid the previous two books in terms of angst, drama, steam, plot twists and had moments of humor that made me laugh ( I am definitely in love wit</span>
  <span id="freeText6033717357533413554" style="display:none"><br><br>5++++ Stars<br><br>Another Trilogy I am sad to see end! Another couple that have cemented themselves as favorites of mine. I love a book that you cannot put down, I was trying to read every chance I get, at work, when I stopped at the traffic lights and definitely did not sleep that night trying to finish it! Yup I was it's bitch!!!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389698327ra/8049029.gif" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>It was amazing, certainly outdid the previous two books in terms of angst, drama, steam, plot twists and had moments of humor that made me laugh ( I am definitely in love with Jack, Hudson's father)...<br><br> <b>“Jack, I have a personal question for you, if you don’t mind.” “About six and a half inches . But it’s not size that matters; it’s what you do with it.”<br><br> Jack cocked his head. “Did he just growl?”</b>“<br><br>Alayna and Hudson are one couple that should not be together yet they are the best thing to have happened to each other. In 'Forever With You', the plot does not drag, no boring bits that are there to fill pages. We finally get closure and learn all of Hudson's secrets, some of these did not endear him to me but he does make up for it at the end and redeems himself in a big way. so all is forgiven! Alayna's vulnerability, raw emotions and struggle not to slip into old habits were hard to read, felt her pain and who could blame her for acting up, Hudson's mysterious actions would have driven anyone into going crazy!<br><br><br><b>Alayna- I loved Hudson Pierce with every fiber of my being. Even his flaws and imperfections attracted me to him. They made him who he was. And I wanted all of him. I wanted to give him all of me.</b><br> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389698327i/8049030._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>We also get a chapter from Hudson's POV, loved it!<br><br><b>Hudson- Whatever it was, there was a definite recognition of her soul by mine. An awareness of something greater that tied us to each other upon first acquaintance.</b><br> <br><br>He was protective, sweet, tender and loving and at times a complete asshole but most of all he was still the same sexy insatiable Hudson!<br><br> <b>Hudson- It will be easier to keep her naked on a private beach than at the site of an ancient ruin or in an art museum.</b> <br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389698327i/8049031.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The epilogue was PERFECTION, I'm going to miss these two, Highly recommend!</span>

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer690800375" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5004181575038332402">(4.5 I Give You All Of Me Stars)<br/>(BR with Patty)<br/><br/><a href='http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/70b4ae98-98e3-4589-b718-51065e1f62ad.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><br/><a href='http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/c82f1191-69a5-4411-bf4c-a2de3202e55d.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389743843i/8052489.jpg' alt=' photo c82f1191-69a5-4411-bf4c-a2de3202e55d.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>In book three Hudson and Laynie are continuing to put their relationship back together. They are committed to each other 100%, but things are still a little rocky. They are trying to learn from their past mistakes, and be open and honest with each other. Laynie really grows in her confidence in this book, but is also extremely annoying at times. Sometimes I wanted to just shake some sense into her.<br/><br/><a href='http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/7a6c475d-dc0d-4633-9596-9822e308f1e5.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389988186i/8120723.jpg' alt=' photo 7a6c475d-dc0d-4633-9596-9822e308f1e5.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>There is plenty of angst, jealousy, and </span>
  <span id="freeText5004181575038332402" style="display:none">(4.5 I Give You All Of Me Stars)<br>(BR with Patty)<br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/70b4ae98-98e3-4589-b718-51065e1f62ad.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389743843i/8052488.jpg" alt=" photo 70b4ae98-98e3-4589-b718-51065e1f62ad.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/c82f1191-69a5-4411-bf4c-a2de3202e55d.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389743843i/8052489.jpg" alt=" photo c82f1191-69a5-4411-bf4c-a2de3202e55d.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>In book three Hudson and Laynie are continuing to put their relationship back together. They are committed to each other 100%, but things are still a little rocky. They are trying to learn from their past mistakes, and be open and honest with each other. Laynie really grows in her confidence in this book, but is also extremely annoying at times. Sometimes I wanted to just shake some sense into her.<br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/7a6c475d-dc0d-4633-9596-9822e308f1e5.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389988186i/8120723.jpg" alt=" photo 7a6c475d-dc0d-4633-9596-9822e308f1e5.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>There is plenty of angst, jealousy, and drama. I continue to want bitch Celia to just fall off a cliff. Secrets explode, and their relationship is challenged, but the one thing that never changes is their love for one another. They really have true, deep feelings for each other, and continue to learn they aren't perfect, but are perfect for each other. They figure out they will do just about anything to be together, and learn to forgive and believe in each other. No matter what happens, they always seem to find their way back to one another.<br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/5f768d93-6b44-43aa-b542-28051d42e4be.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389745843i/8052706.jpg" alt=" photo 5f768d93-6b44-43aa-b542-28051d42e4be.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Hudson Pierce continues to be my favorite thing about this series! He is still delicious as ever and I just can't help but love him! The way he fights for her was just swoon worthy! I thought this was a wonderful conclusion to the series, and an absolutely beautiful HEA! <br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/0b1ee5fa-963e-4e18-bb72-1cb82eb9f0be.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389988186i/8120724.jpg" alt=" photo 0b1ee5fa-963e-4e18-bb72-1cb82eb9f0be.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>-He was such an expert at handling me in the way I needed, his touch never too gentle, always just the right amount of rough.<br><br>-At his own pace, Hudson took me to where I wanted and needed to go. Loving me thoroughly with his body. Loving me entirely without words. Loving me completely.<br><br>-I slid my gaze over him. He was so hot. I didn't think I could ever get tired of how delicious his body was. And he was all mine.<br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/95417736-3505-4b2a-997c-0b2d298e891e.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389745843i/8052707.jpg" alt=" photo 95417736-3505-4b2a-997c-0b2d298e891e.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>-"Anything you want, Alayna. It's yours.<br><br>-"You're the center of my world, precious. Every minute of every day. Even when I'm not with you." He brushed his lips against mine. </a><br><br>-He was so deeply imprinted on me that he'd seeped through my skin and into my veins. He was my life force, each pulse of my heart sending another shock of love through my body.<br><br>-Our eyes locked, and the intensity of his expression- it was all-consuming. Maybe I couldn't read all of my own emotions, but in his gaze I saw three with clarity. Surprise, elation. And, clear as day, I saw love.<br><br>-His touch was searing, his kiss burned me to my core. And the solidness of his body, his strong arms, his muscled chest- he was my foundation. Sturdy and fixed. Permanent.<br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/4d088267-6490-4bbb-8fa6-d756a5a468d9.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>-Hudson Pierce naked. I had to swallow. Twice. There wasn't any sight on Earth that compared to the mouth-watering deliciousness in front of me. And it was all mine.<br><br>-Whatever it was, there was a definite recognition of her soul by mine. An awareness of something greater that tied us to each other upon first acquaintance. As if some part of me had always known she was out there, had been waiting for her to come and bring me to life.<br><br></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer821871716" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17083423761005743599">5 *'s or more! I am beyond happy with the conclusion for Hudson and Alayna...Laurelin Paige knocked this out!<br/><br/><b>"Where is the road to your heart?"...With one finger he lifted my chin to meet his eyes. "Dont you know" You're the one who paved it."</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389744608i/8052540._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Yay, total swoon! I freely admit that Alayna Withers is NUTS...she is crazy obsessive, insecure, and often stupid, but for some reason H loves her. Yep, he even says so for the first time, and he continues to say it making my heart swell. She could have eas</span>
  <span id="freeText17083423761005743599" style="display:none">5 *'s or more! I am beyond happy with the conclusion for Hudson and Alayna...Laurelin Paige knocked this out!<br><br><b>"Where is the road to your heart?"...With one finger he lifted my chin to meet his eyes. "Dont you know" You're the one who paved it."</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389744608i/8052540._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Yay, total swoon! I freely admit that Alayna Withers is NUTS...she is crazy obsessive, insecure, and often stupid, but for some reason H loves her. Yep, he even says so for the first time, and he continues to say it making my heart swell. She could have easily made me hate this series, especially since her wackiness is over the top here, but who am i to argue with who H loves? Also, Celia Werner is still present, still a complete bitch and she is pure evil, so i felt for Alayna!<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389744608i/8052541.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So, I put the crazy aside and said YES to loving Hudson and the tale that was woven into their lives. There has always been a sense of unease to this read, a true longing for goodness. I have felt mind f***'d from book one, no wander Alayna was so edgy and compulsive! I only ever felt at ease when they were wrapped in each other...and they do it so damn well<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389744608i/8052542._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>"He'd never let anyone in before, Maybe sex really had only been for sport in the past. With us it was speech."</b><br><br>So, finally an answer to the main question I have had in the back of my mind from book 1, was Hudson playing a game? Well, you are going to have to read to find that out! I was a bit emotionally rocked by the answer! I applaud the character transformation as Alayna grew spine and Hudson grew heart. I also applaud he conclusion that was no let down, and I mostly applaud the continued heat and fire that never fizzled from book 1.<br><br>Hudson Pierce, I put you in my top 5 book boyfriend as i will definitely go back and re-read those "i love yous" "i need yous" and "you are my worlds" that came out of your beautiful mouth!<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389744608i/8052543.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer716571098" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer8118098944123753277">Dear Lord that was a train wreck. <br/><br/>I had such high hopes with this series when I read book 1. Yes they had issues but instead of getting better together they continued to fuck up every day! It's like 1 day couldn't go by with no drama. <br/><br/>This latest installment was no different. They solved everything with sex. Alayna was a whiney little bitch. Hudson with held information and refused to tell her. Even then she begged him to stay?! Say goodbye and grow some balls, woman! <br/><br/>Celia? She was the issue wi</span>
  <span id="freeText8118098944123753277" style="display:none">Dear Lord that was a train wreck. <br /><br />I had such high hopes with this series when I read book 1. Yes they had issues but instead of getting better together they continued to fuck up every day! It's like 1 day couldn't go by with no drama. <br /><br />This latest installment was no different. They solved everything with sex. Alayna was a whiney little bitch. Hudson with held information and refused to tell her. Even then she begged him to stay?! Say goodbye and grow some balls, woman! <br /><br />Celia? She was the issue with all 3 books. Zero originality. At least bring something fresh to the table. <br /><br />When the truth came out it was that Hudson started the relationship with her as a game with Celia. <br />FINALLY Alayna tells him to leave. Well thank God! She finally grew a pair. What does she do after crying for days? Goes to his loft to smell his sheets. You have got to be kidding me. Chick is fucked. <br /><br />I will say the only thing that sorta saved this book was Hudson groveling. He did do a good grovel. <br /><br />I know this review is all over the place but I just finished reading and it's all rambling in my head.<br /><br />On a whole I'm not impressed with the series. It was drawn out and repeatative. </span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1656658939" />
    <a title="Mindy Lou&#39;s Book Review" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/44132489-mindy-lou-s-book-review"><img alt="Mindy Lou&#39;s Book Review" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1465424458p2/44132489.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/25967057-forever-with-you">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44132489-mindy-lou-s-book-review?shelf=my-kind-of-alpha">my-kind-of-alpha</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44132489-mindy-lou-s-book-review?shelf=2015">2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44132489-mindy-lou-s-book-review?shelf=2017">2017</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44132489-mindy-lou-s-book-review?shelf=audible-owned">audible-owned</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44132489-mindy-lou-s-book-review?shelf=re-reads">re-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44132489-mindy-lou-s-book-review?shelf=grovel">grovel</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1656658939" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5266454583988601292"><b>Audible Review:</b> I did a re-listen when I bought the audible companion. I still stand on my review below and I think everyone will enjoy this narrator. I had no issues distinguishing between characters. I would buy more audibles with her as a narrator.<br/><br/><b>Story Review:</b> This series is going into my list of top favorites. The way this story unfolded with all the crazy actions of these equally crazy people just had me completely hooked. I enjoyed trying to figure out truth from all the secrets, lies and</span>
  <span id="freeText5266454583988601292" style="display:none"><b>Audible Review:</b> I did a re-listen when I bought the audible companion. I still stand on my review below and I think everyone will enjoy this narrator. I had no issues distinguishing between characters. I would buy more audibles with her as a narrator.<br /><br /><b>Story Review:</b> This series is going into my list of top favorites. The way this story unfolded with all the crazy actions of these equally crazy people just had me completely hooked. I enjoyed trying to figure out truth from all the secrets, lies and sabotage. Plus, there were so many side characters that added life to this story.<br /><br />While I thought Alayna was way too needy, I still rooted for her. Her neediness was a huge part of the plot and why things went down the way they did. Despite the fact that I probably shouldn't have liked Hudson for his past, I actually loved him! I'm really looking forward to reading his book to get his POV. There were so many times when I wasn't sure of what was real when it came to him. <br /><br />Celia is the one side character that deserves honorable mention. I predicted I wanted to shove her off a cliff in the first book and that still stands. Wow, what a conniving woman! Normally I hate other women drama, but I think this author did her part extremely well and it's obvious, her role is very necessary to the overall plot. <br /><br />I highly recommend this series. Just be ready to go on a ride!</span>

<div id="review_733365937" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/733365937" />
    <a title="Mirjana **DTR - Down to Read**" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3068938-mirjana-dtr---down-to-read"><img alt="Mirjana **DTR - Down to Read**" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1504717217p2/3068938.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/733365937?book_show_action=true">Oct 03, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mirjana **DTR - Down to Read**" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mirjana **DTR - Down to Read**" href="/user/show/3068938-mirjana-dtr---down-to-read">Mirjana **DTR - Down to Read**</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3068938-mirjana-dtr---down-to-read?shelf=4-star">4-star</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3068938-mirjana-dtr---down-to-read?shelf=i-m-broken">i-m-broken</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3068938-mirjana-dtr---down-to-read?shelf=mo-money-mo-problems">mo-money-mo-problems</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3068938-mirjana-dtr---down-to-read?shelf=talk-dirty-to-me">talk-dirty-to-me</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3068938-mirjana-dtr---down-to-read?shelf=guuurrrrll">guuurrrrll</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3068938-mirjana-dtr---down-to-read?shelf=paperbacks">paperbacks</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer733365937" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18285514363366735004"><br/><b>***3.75 Stars***</b><br/><br/>I couldn't wait to see how Alayna and Hudson's story ended....Unfortunately, the final book in this series has left me a bit disappointed. <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1400331625ra/9663581.gif' width='261' height='227' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Before I begin with my issues, I want to say that regardless of them, I still couldn't put my kindle down and devoured the book in a day.<br/><br/>Alayna's issues drove me crazy! All the strength I though she had in the first book slowly drifted away with each passing paragraph. She wasn't sharing what she was feeling. She was getting more and more para</span>
  <span id="freeText18285514363366735004" style="display:none"><br><b>***3.75 Stars***</b><br><br>I couldn't wait to see how Alayna and Hudson's story ended....Unfortunately, the final book in this series has left me a bit disappointed. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1400331625ra/9663581.gif" width="261" height="227" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Before I begin with my issues, I want to say that regardless of them, I still couldn't put my kindle down and devoured the book in a day.<br><br>Alayna's issues drove me crazy! All the strength I though she had in the first book slowly drifted away with each passing paragraph. She wasn't sharing what she was feeling. She was getting more and more paranoid, jealous and obsessive with her behavior. And her reasoning was manipulative....which is kind of ironic since that was suppose to be Hudson's department. As the book wore on, I found I had a mantra when it came to Alayna...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1405908956ra/10469989.gif" width="250" height="190" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>However, Hudson holds some blame as well. Keeping such a big secret from Alayna, which could have been resolved with a heartfelt conversation earlier in their relationship, was definitely not cool. And due to his fear, he kept dismissing Alayna's concerns and refused to talk to her about very important issues. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1405908956ra/10469990.gif" width="480" height="276" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>With regards to the big reveal: I feel like Alayna WAY over-reacted. She didn't allow Hudson to explain himself AT ALL. If she would have pulled her head out of her ass long enough to hear him out, he would have been able to explain and ultimately apologize, for not telling her sooner. The majority of his actions were easily seen and felt as sincere, but she was so distraught by the "betrayal" that she couldn't see around it. I think maybe I was just fed up with her at that point that I couldn't feel too bad. He had caught her in the arms of a man that they both knew, and had acknowledged, was in love with her. She knew it was wrong to dance with him....and then to even put herself in the situation that he would have the opportunity to kiss her. WRONG!! If she had caught Hudson in that same situation with ANYONE, she would have flipped her lid! But without her distraught behavior, then we couldn't have been set up with pages and pages of Hudson groveling. Ok, rant over. <br><br>A large part of my frustration with this final installment could have been solved with dual POV's. Being solely in Alayna's head made me feel slightly OCD myself. But I am happy that we got a glimpse inside of Hudson's head in the epilogue. <br><br>Also, sex doesn't solve everything. These two were fucking like rabbits instead of talking their issues out. And the moment they'd start getting somewhere, ooops out comes Hudson's cock and oooops there goes Alayna's brain function. I'm thinking Alayna should have used her rubberband technique when she was overcome with lust. Just a reminder, <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1405908956ra/10469991.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Talk things out first. Sex is the reward....not the solution.<br><br>Overall, this was a series that started strong, but ultimately lost its luster in increments with each passing book. Though the characters and story frustrated me, I have definitely become a fan of Laurelin Paige's writing. She created memorable characters (loved Jack's dirty sense of humor and Mira was unbelievably endearing....let's not forget crazy bi-curious Lisle!) and an intriguing spin to what could have been a cliched story. <br><br>I'm off to find out what Hudson has to say about all of this. I really need to see what was going through his head and why he acted the way he did in certain circumstances. And for the love of God, why was he friends with Celia!! </span>
  <a data-text-id="18285514363366735004" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <a title="Amanda" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7451210-amanda"><img alt="Amanda" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1434101513p2/7451210.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/821613749?book_show_action=true">Jan 12, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Amanda" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Amanda" href="/user/show/7451210-amanda">Amanda</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7451210-amanda?shelf=favourite-2014">favourite-2014</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7451210-amanda?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer821613749" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5970019135152400912">What a load of clusterfuck moments we had here. This book make me annoyed, angry, frustrated, infuriated and basically wanted to strangle fictional people or maybe I need a really strong drink. I might just end up being Sophia's drinking buddy. <br/><br/>I've read all 3 books back to back and this one was the one with the most revelation and WTF moment. Remember Stacy who wanted to show Laynie a video of Hudson? I'm dying to uncover what was this big secret that Hudson was hiding. Laynie and Hudson was al</span>
  <span id="freeText5970019135152400912" style="display:none">What a load of clusterfuck moments we had here. This book make me annoyed, angry, frustrated, infuriated and basically wanted to strangle fictional people or maybe I need a really strong drink. I might just end up being Sophia's drinking buddy. <br /><br />I've read all 3 books back to back and this one was the one with the most revelation and WTF moment. Remember Stacy who wanted to show Laynie a video of Hudson? I'm dying to uncover what was this big secret that Hudson was hiding. Laynie and Hudson was also dealing with this psychotic Celia who was set to destroy both of them. With so much drama going on, I wanted the secret to be something huge and epic. Well, as it turn out it was not as epic as I had imagine, but it kinda make sense and it explains a lot. It makes me wanna reread Book 1 in a different view.<br /><br />This started off with much sweetness and hotness. Laynie and Hudson was so in love. For once, Laynie wanted to come clean and she insist on transparency and trust. Hudson agreed. They both fully committed to each other.<br /><br /><b>"This is better than a beginning. This is what happens next."</b><br /><br />But it was obvious Hudson was still hiding something. Even though how hard he tried to convince her that he loves her and nothing else matter, to Laynie everything matters. She wanted to get inside him and know everything about him. Well, they said curiosity kills the cat. It might just be true.<br /><br />Before I tried making this sounds like angst overload, there were lots of hotness and humor in it too. I will repeat once again, their sex scenes were freaking hot, no matter the location.<br /><br /><b>"Jesus, now I'm hard again."<br />"Are you kidding me?"<br />"No. I'm not."<br />"I saw Celia."<br />"And now I'm soft."</b><br /><br />I thought Laynie would finally morph into this strong heroine in Book 3, but she was still this person who was constantly at edge, paranoid, suspicious and her curiosity might just ruined everything. I know, I know, Hudson was at fault too. But from my perspective as Laynie's first person POV, she was overly suspicious and totally double standard in regards the Hudson. She kept going on and on about Norma and Hudson had to repeatedly reassured her, but it seems like everything fall on deaf ears. Have she seen the way she was with David? Urg! Double standard much? <br /><br />Nevertheless, I don't why that no matter how much I'm pissed at Laynie, I still rooting for her. If it was any other book, I would have DNF long ago.<br /><br />I had big crush on Hudson Pierce since book 1. He was an enigma, elusive and complicated, and I wanted to know everything about him. He was sexy and domineering when it comes to Laynie. I don't know what kind of trance he put on me because I was totally soaking up his every words. <br /><br /><b>Now kiss me because you've made me a very happy man."</b><br /><br />Now that we knew the truth, should I hate him? Maybe I should, but I don't. If Laynie was the perfect heroine, maybe I will asked her to dump his sorry ass, no matter how hard he grovel. But since Laynie was such an imperfect heroine and I really felt the sincerity in Hudson to make things right, I thought they both were made for each other. You get my drill? For those who want to know whether was there any cheating involved. Answer is <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[no! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />For all the frustration I had while reading this series. It was superbly addictive and entertaining. It was a great ending for Laynie and Hudson. I hate them. I love them. We had a nice little epilogue from Hudson's POV. The next book will be on Gwen, Laynie's new assistant manager at the club. </span>
  <a data-text-id="5970019135152400912" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>
