<div id="review_686513084" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/686513084" />
    <a title="Lisa" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13978199-lisa"><img alt="Lisa" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1412857185p2/13978199.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/686513084?book_show_action=true">Aug 05, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lisa" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lisa" href="/user/show/13978199-lisa">Lisa</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13978199-lisa?shelf=angsty-romance">angsty-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13978199-lisa?shelf=dying-to-get-my-hands-on">dying-to-get-my-hands-on</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13978199-lisa?shelf=suits">suits</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13978199-lisa?shelf=arc-given-to-blog-for-honest-review">arc-given-to-blog-for-honest-review</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13978199-lisa?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13978199-lisa?shelf=fav-books-of-all-time">fav-books-of-all-time</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13978199-lisa?shelf=beta">beta</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13978199-lisa?shelf=read-in-2013">read-in-2013</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer686513084" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14354760140937068841">*ARC Given to Blog for Honest Review*<br/><br/>5+++++ <b> “Precious” <i> “So Easy” “All of Me” </i> “Without struggle there is no progress” </b> Kisses!<br/><br/>OMG I need more stars…5 isn’t enough. I need like a million stars…a trillion…maybe infinity. Because <b>that’s</b> what Hudson and Laynie are worth. If I thought I loved them before this book, <i>Forever With You</i> just sent me into another realm of love. This series is and always will be one of my favorite’s of all time. Hudson and Laynie…their story…their passion…their emotions…t</span>
  <span id="freeText14354760140937068841" style="display:none">*ARC Given to Blog for Honest Review*<br><br>5+++++ <b> “Precious” <i> “So Easy” “All of Me” </i> “Without struggle there is no progress” </b> Kisses!<br><br>OMG I need more stars…5 isn’t enough. I need like a million stars…a trillion…maybe infinity. Because <b>that’s</b> what Hudson and Laynie are worth. If I thought I loved them before this book, <i>Forever With You</i> just sent me into another realm of love. This series is and always will be one of my favorite’s of all time. Hudson and Laynie…their story…their passion…their emotions…their love…will forever be ingrained in my heart. Now if you have absolutely no idea what or who I am talking about, you must drop everything <i>immediately</i> and read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/601702978" rel="nofollow noopener">Fixed On You</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/686513078" rel="nofollow noopener"> Found In You</a>, the first two books in the Fixed Trilogy. This is a series that must be read in order…and believe me when I say you <b>have</b> to read it.<br><br>Alayna Withers…oh my Laynie girl…each book she has consistently shown me how strong she is. How she is not the sum of her past but is capable of so much more. Her strength surpassed my highest expectations because trust me…she is tested consistently through <i>FWY</i>…and every time I was cheering her on. The simple fact of the matter is…she has her dream. Her dream life…dream job…dream apartment…and most of all dream man. A man that by all accounts should be running from her and her past...but he’s not. He’s crazy about her…all of her, even the crazier parts of her…which kind of makes them this crazy couple and it's so endearing and totally makes me love them even more. But what I admired most about Laynie in <i>FWY</i> was her persistence in making her and Hudson better together…keeping the truth, honesty and trust in the forefront of their relationship…being stronger and better together. Because in all honesty that are <b>so</b> much better when they are together.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431877i/866875._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><blockquote> <b> “We both have to change. We have to put everything out on the line, Hudson, as much as possible. We know now that we’re together, thick and thin, right? We have to trust that more than anything. We can’t be afraid of our secrets and our pasts. Both of us. Honesty, open doors, transparency.” </b> </blockquote><br>Hudson Alexander Pierce…yeah…it’s official…one of my top book bf’s of all time. I claim him for all eternity and he might be edging his way up into the ‘Book Husband’ seat. That’s how much I love me some H. He. Blew. Me. Away. Like all of the love I developed him over the course of the past two books…roll that up into a ball, multiply it by 10, send it to the moon and back and then you might have a tenth of my love for him. Why? Because…ladies and gents – we finally get to see behind the curtain. We <i>finally</i> get to see <b>THE</b> Hudson Pierce…stripped bare with emotions for all the world to see. There are no secrets, there is no wondering ‘<i> what if he’s lying</i>’…and I ate it up like a bowlful of the most delicious ice cream in the world. Hudson flavored ice cream…with chocolate sauce and a cherry on top. Or maybe that was just my fantasy…oh well – moving on! I always had faith in Hudson and while I may have been wary…I never lost that faith…because I knew he was capable of amazing things. And I was right.<br><br><blockquote> <b> ‘I twisted my lips at the thought. “This is a new beginning for us, isn’t it?”<br>He leaned forward to brush my nose with his. “No. This is better than a beginning. This is what happens next.”<br>“I like that.”<br>He leaned in and kissed me, sweet and luxuriously, with promises of all the other things that would happen next. As if there was nothing in the world to do but lavish me with love.’ </b> </blockquote><br>Of course <i>FWY</i> is packed full of all the things I <b>L-O-V-E-D</b> in <i>FOY</i> and <i>FIY</i>. The first one being the never-ending gloriously perfect, leave you panting and begging for more delightfully sinful hot sex scenes. That is part of what makes Hudson and Laynie, Hudson and Laynie. Their sexual connection and physical chemistry is what made me love them to begin with and honestly, what solidifies them as a couple in my mind. That is not to discount anything else that they have…their devotion and feelings about each other are clear in everything that they do but the way they show their love is never more clear than with sex. That’s their strongest bond…their deepest connection and I thrive on it. I make it no secret that I’m a dirty book whore lovin' gal and the Fixed series as a whole has totally and completely satisfied me in that regards…by far. But <i>FWY</i> surpassed that by leaps and bounds…in every book Hudson and Laynie’s love scene’s have always blown my mind but there was just something about this book that wow’d me. Maybe it was because I could almost feel Laynie and Hudson’s feelings about each other…that made it better…more meaningful…knowing the struggle and what it has taken to get them to this point…it made it that much more special.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389575428ra/8041338.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote> <b> ‘It had been true for me. Until him, sex had been fun, but that’s all. Sometimes it could even begin an unhealthy obsession. But it was never about the physical. With Hudson it wasn’t exactly about the sex, either. It was more about wanting to be as close to him as possible. And, especially because it was how he communicated best, that involved being naked.<br>He’d never let anyone in before. Maybe sex really had only been for sport in the past. With us, it was speech.’ </b> </blockquote><br>So…I wish I could say Laynie and Hudson got through <b>all</b> the drama of the last two books to just have the little details to work through on <i>FWY</i>…that there is no stress…no anxiety…no worry…no drama…just focus on some good quality L&amp;H time and it’s easy peasy lemon squeezy. Yeah…freaking…right. There is way too much that has been building up this might be the <b>most</b> stressful of the three books…but for me it was for different reasons. I <b>knew</b> that whatever was on that videotape was going to be bad. I <b>knew</b> that Celia wasn’t going to go away quietly. I <b>knew</b> that Laynie and Hudson had a shit load of stuff to get through before they would get their HEA. And I <b>knew</b> that Hudson might break my heart a little bit. <b>But</b> I also knew that no matter what happened…Hudson could be redeemed. And I was glad I was right about that.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389575428ra/8041339.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote> <b> He yanked me closer to him. “That was <i>for us</i>.” His eyes widened as he emphasized the last two words. “Have I done anything that makes you think I don’t have our relationship’s best interests in mind? Have I done anything to make you believe that I don’t want to be with you? That I don’t…” His voice cracked and he swallowed before continuing. “That I don’t <i>care</i>…for you with everything I have?”<br>I shook my head, unable to speak.<br>He relaxed his grasp on me, but didn’t let go. “Everything I’ve done since we’ve been together has been for you and me. Trust me when I tell you this isn’t important.” With his free hand, he brushed my hair off my shoulder. “This doesn’t affect us.” </b> </blockquote><br>The truth is and was a lot harder to accept and take than I thought it would be. Okay that’s putting it nicely…I was crush. I cried…I hated it…I hated the pain that both of them were going through but my heart broke for Laynie. Her agony is soul-crushing and I felt it. I understood it. I hated every minute of it <i>but</i>, and this is an important but…I didn’t not hate Hudson. I didn’t like what was happening…I didn’t want it to be true…but like Laynie, I think a part of me has known for a while and didn’t really want to admit it. Denial is a wonderful thing. I do think everything that happened from the point that Laynie finds out the truth to the end was absolutely necessary in Hudson and Laynie’s journey. It wasn’t pretty…it wasn’t all fun and games…but it was crucial to getting them where they needed to be. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380417601ra/826176.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote> <b> “No, I’m not ever letting you go.” His words were raw with emotion. “I’ll let you leave here right now, but I’m not giving up on you. I’ll pursue you like I’ve never pursued anything in my life. I’ll fight until you have no choice to believe that I love you with everything I am.” </b> </blockquote><br>For the record…Celia is a crazy ass biatch and is going on my list of ‘Evil Wenches in Books’ (joining the ranks of Bekah and Leah)…she is evil and must be destroyed…but there is a particularly awesome scene in which I kind of want to high five Laynie for her actions. There were some things that surprised me…like how much of a part Hudson’s family plays in this book. I absolutely adore Mira to bits…she’s amazing. Another shocker…I was actually really worried about Sophia and her possible role in this book…but her part is actually quite…interesting. Unexpected and yet fitting…and I mean that in the best way possible for a character that I really can’t stand. There are some new players added which I did enjoy <b>very</b> much…Norma and Gwen. They are sisters and each one plays their part in how things…develop, plot wise…and it’s definitely not what I expected. Oh and I might love Liesl more than I really should. She was <b>amazing</b> to Laynie…absolutely fabulous friend and on top of that she made me laugh so many times it got to be ridiculous.<br><br><blockquote> <b> ‘The reason to accept was because I loved Hudson Pierce with every fiber of my being. Even his flaws and imperfections attracted me to him. They made him who he was. And I wanted all of him. I wanted to give him all of me.<br>And he had a lot of making up to do to me. Forever might just be the only way he’d get it covered.’ </b> </blockquote><br>The ending is…just wow. I feel like for those last few pages Laynie and Hudson held my heart in their hands. I knew what I wanted to do…what I wanted Laynie to do…and what I hope Hudson would say and do. I just hoped and prayed that all of that happened and worked out. And it did. But do you want to know the best part of <i>FWY</i>? The mother loving <b>BEST</b> epilogue in the history of epilogues. Ever. You heard it here first. Want to know why? Two words. Well…actually 1 word and 3 letters…<b>Hudson’s POV</b>! <i>BOOM</i>! Best thing <b>ever</b>. OMG…there are no words for my emotions when I realized I was reading his POV…there was <i>squee</i>'ing and clapping and the biggest goofiest grin on my face! How can a POV make me so happy? I don't know but straight up, in Hudson's brain is where I need to move if those are the emotions that are elicited from my body. And then it got better. Because…the last chapter of <i>FWY</i> is not the end. Things are not complete in the world of Hudson and Laynie until you read that epilogue and know the whole story. The epilogue <b>makes</b> the book for me…and for more reasons than the fact that it was in his POV.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386101873ra/7292037.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote> <b> ‘I nip at her ear. “Oh, precious, I’m very resourceful. Need I remind you I’m a man who gets what I want?” Again I lean back to look in her eyes. “And anyone who ever doubted that only needs to look at me right now to know it’s true. Everything I want is here, in my arms.”<br>“I love you,” she murmurs.<br>“I love you first.” And last. And everything in between.’ </b> </blockquote><br>I hate that to think that it’s over…that this is the last book that I will read in the Fixed Series. I refuse to admit that Laynie and Hudson’s story is over…not because it doesn’t feel over or complete…because it does…but because I don’t want to let them go. I love them so much…Laynie is fabulous, Hudson is a dream and I want to throw a temper tantrum because I can’t say goodbye. *insert 4-year-old whiney fit here* I will beg and plead for more…especially more of Hudson’s POV ;-) But even if we get Gwen or Norma’s story…or even Chandler – I’ll take the option to fall in love with another Pierce man…I’m sure he can be just as much fun as Hudson. Alright…I’m getting desperate – this is what this series has done to me! Do <b>not</b> hesitate to read this series…it’s amazing! Emotion packed, sexy as hell, fantastic writing and engaging characters...one of the best series I’ve ever read, hands down. Just…<b>yes</b>! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389575428i/8041340._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380434116i/874066.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380434116i/874067.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="14354760140937068841" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer678833809" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14001203058235583535">5+++ Beautiful, Heartbreaking, Sexy Stars!<br/><br/>Happy Release Day! As Promised this is the full review!<br/><br/>5+++ Emotional, Sexy, Heartbreaking Stars!<br/><br/>“You’re the center of my world, precious. Every minute of every day. Even when I’m not with you.” He brushed his lips against mine. “You make it so easy to fall so hard.” ~Hudson Pierce<br/><br/>I have read, adored, obsessed over, and pimped this series since the beginning. Alayna and Hudson have become one of my all-time favourite book couples. I fell head over heels </span>
  <span id="freeText14001203058235583535" style="display:none">5+++ Beautiful, Heartbreaking, Sexy Stars!<br /><br />Happy Release Day! As Promised this is the full review!<br /><br />5+++ Emotional, Sexy, Heartbreaking Stars!<br /><br />“You’re the center of my world, precious. Every minute of every day. Even when I’m not with you.” He brushed his lips against mine. “You make it so easy to fall so hard.” ~Hudson Pierce<br /><br />I have read, adored, obsessed over, and pimped this series since the beginning. Alayna and Hudson have become one of my all-time favourite book couples. I fell head over heels with these two flawed and broken characters back in Fixed on You. My love has grown and I am so incredibly sad that this is the end of their story. Forever with You is the best in this series by far. This is without a doubt Laurelin Paige’s best work to date, no question. Forever with You, is my first favourite for 2014 and my last favourite of 2013 however you care to look at it. For me it will sit in both categories.<br /><br />Alayna and Hudson are living together at The Bowery as a couple and working on a healthy, honest relationship. Celia is still breathing, sadly, and determined to wreak havoc and destroy their relationship. That wench is seriously determined and evil. Sophia is still a wicked witch, who spends 24/7 at the bottom of a bottle. However Alayna is finally fighting back. This line made me full on belly laugh. I laughed, because I have been planning Celia’s death myself, since Fixed on You. I have imagined a fiery car crash millions of times taking out this B*tch!<br /><br />“It was a good thing I’m a pacifist, because otherwise I’d have to start planning her murder.” ~ Alayna<br /><br />We still have no idea what is on this video that Stacy is determined to share with Alayna. However even with all of this taking place, trust, honesty, and faith in each other’s love and devotion are the true obstacles, in my opinion. I became incredibly frustrated with both Alayna and Hudson in this book. Alayna preaching and pleading with Hudson for complete transparency and honesty. Yet once again she is still hiding things, and putting herself at risk. <br /><br />"We both have to change Hudson. We have to put everything out on the line, Hudson, as much as possible. We know now that we’re together, thick and thin, right? We have to trust that more than anything. We can’t be afraid of our secrets and our pasts. Both of us. Honesty, open doors, transparency.” ~Alayna~<br /><br />Then we have Hudson. Not being able to communicate with Alayna, how he truly feels about her, and still hiding his past. The frustration I felt while reading Forever with You, was a huge part of the experience for me. I had so many reactions and emotions while reading this one, I had emotional whiplash. In the end a crippling hangover. I cursed, cried, laughed, swooned, sighed, cried, cursed, threw things, swooned, sighed, purred, and then cried some more. You know how that is right? Please tell me as readers, you have been there?<br /><br /> This is a new beginning for us, isn’t it?” He leaned forward to brush my nose with his. “No. This is better than a beginning. This is what happens next.” ~Alayna and Hudson~<br /><br />As the story progressed and all secrets and lies are revealed, I broke. I broke with Hudson and Alayna, and I cried. Oh I full on ugly cried. I didn’t think I could finish. I had help and support to talk me off the ledge. I have become so invested and attached to these characters, I may require therapy. Laurlein has sucked me into these stories so completely, I tell myself, “They’re characters, they’re not real, it’ll all be okay. It’ll be okay.”<br /><br />“It would be so easy – so easy to lean up and let him kiss away my pain and insecurity. His lips on mine could erase all darkness, could soothe any pain. Until that afternoon, I’d believed that like some people believed in their religion – Hudson could fix me, every time.” ~Alayna~<br /><br />The writing is beautiful and poetic. It’s clear and concise, never redundant. The flow is flawless. The sexy time scenes are incredible, erotic, and tingle inducing. Romantic and written with an emotional hand. WARNING - You will once again need a fan! I never once wanted it to end; I wanted it to go on forever, minus the frustration of course. It is a fabulous and heartbreaking conclusion to Alayna and Hudson’s story. This series is and always will be on my all-time favourites list, and Laurelin Paige will remain one of my all-time favourite authors. If you have not read this series, do yourself a huge favor and do it. The Fixed Series is a must read for all readers who adore emotional, sexy, beautiful love stories. On that note, I will leave you with my favorite passage from Forever with You.<br /><br />“Afterward, I stood with a towel wrapped around myself and stared into the steam-clouded mirror. This is was what it was like to see Hudson now, through this fog, knowing that something more lay underneath. If only it were as simple as stretching my hand out and wiping away the condensation to see the man beneath. If only he’d let me in, maybe it would be that easy. Maybe then my touch could finally bring him into focus.” – Alayna, Laurelin Paige, Forever with You<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="14001203058235583535" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2993131111" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2639552395939341800"><b>4.5 "2 parts mind game, add in 1 crazy bitch" stars</b><br/><br/>This is the third book in what was originally the Fixed Trilogy but is now a 5-books series -- and thank goodness! because while I was racing through this book with my anxiety working overtime, I would have been bummed to have to say goodbye to these two hot messes just yet. None of the books in this series are standalones, so if you haven't read Fixed on You and Found in You, do not read this one yet because you will be hella lost! Also, please</span>
  <span id="freeText2639552395939341800" style="display:none"><b>4.5 "2 parts mind game, add in 1 crazy bitch" stars</b><br /><br />This is the third book in what was originally the Fixed Trilogy but is now a 5-books series -- and thank goodness! because while I was racing through this book with my anxiety working overtime, I would have been bummed to have to say goodbye to these two hot messes just yet. None of the books in this series are standalones, so if you haven't read Fixed on You and Found in You, do not read this one yet because you will be hella lost! Also, please note that this review contains spoilers if you have not read the previous books.<br /><br />When we last left Hudson (smoking hot rich dude who plays people in both business and relationships for kicks) and Alayna, aka Laynie (stunning/model-esque night club manager who falls hard, fast, and sometimes illegally), they had weathered some pretty big trust issues with each other but still have a ways to go. While Laynie's problem is rooted in her insecurity, Hudson is extremely possessive. Their respective work places involve members of the opposite sex that each has some suspicion about (H: <i>David seems way too cozy with Laynie... I'll just transfer him to a location a couple hundred miles away...</i> L: <i>Norma is checking Hudson out way too much, and they are working long hours on a "special project," so I will flip out on Hudson for the 400th time this week about this when I "accidentally" check his phone and see he called her late one night.</i>). These are not the poster children for functional relationships. Now add Hudson's crazy ex-but-not-really-an-ex-but-maybe-an-ex-but-maybe-not Celia to the mix who has decided to stalk Laynie (something Laynie herself did at the conclusion of some of her past romantic entanglements) and you have something combustible. Add another one of Hudson's scorned women who has "proof" that Celia isn't an ex, and Laynie is practically certifiable. When she confronts Hudson with her fears, he assures her all is well, but when she finds out he is still hiding something and confronts him, he is unwilling to budge. Is this the end for our mutually obsessed couple? How can they possibly fully trust each other if the cards aren't all on the table? And once they are laid bare, can their relationship survive the fall out?<br /><br />What I liked:<br />--- Hudson has been a straight up cold a-hole in most of his relationships, but Laynie has brought the best out of him in this one -- he's borderline mushy at times!<br />--- Laynie is described as insanely gorgeous, but her psychosis makes her much more human and relatable<br />--- STEAMY goodness! Not just the presence of it, but the descriptions - not in a graphic way, but if you have ever been in a passionate relationship where you are basically certain one of you will likely inhale the other by accident, you get it<br />--- Interesting story line that keeps the pages turning quickly<br /><br />What I didn't like as much:<br />--- There was more angst than I typically like, especially when <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[the "big" secret is revealed that was entirely obvious at a certain point and should not have been a surprise to Laynie but inexplicably was <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br />--- Frustrating when they don't communicate<br /><br />Overall, another delicious read with plenty of steam, twists, crazy moments, and strong plot line. So happy there is a book 4 (and that it is told in Hudson's POV!)!<br /><br />Plot --- 4.5/5<br />Main Characters --- 4.5/5<br />Supporting Cast --- 4/5<br />Steam Level* --- 4/5<br />Violence --- none<br />Language --- the f word makes appearances early &amp; often<br />POV --- 1st (Laynie's POV; Brief Epilogue in Hudson's)<br /><br />*Note that steam level is not a rating so much as a how hot was it: 0/5 - clean; 1/5 - mild; 2/5 - sensual but nothing descriptive; 3/5 - now we're getting somewhere; 4/5 - yes please! ; 5/5 - they did EVERYTHING in this one, y'all</span>
  <a data-text-id="2639552395939341800" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_680404577" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/680404577" />
    <a title="Chandra" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10010878-chandra"><img alt="Chandra" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1397788560p2/10010878.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/680404577?book_show_action=true">Jul 29, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Chandra" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Chandra" href="/user/show/10010878-chandra">Chandra</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10010878-chandra?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer680404577" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15795938542373963434"><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1390070552ra/8138415.gif' width='400' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>**May Contain Spoilers**<br/><br/>Story Rating 4.5 Stars<br/>Hero Rating 5 Stars <br/>Heroine Rating 4 Stars<br/>Romance Rating 4.5 Stars<br/>Heat Level 5 Stars<br/>Overall Rating 4.5 Stars</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1390070552ra/8138416.gif' width='400' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I realized after I finished this book, that I haven’t written a review for ANY of the books in the series (not even as casting!), and I think the last one deserves a little something. <i>Not</i> that my reviews are literary masterpieces, but I did love this series, so...here goes.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389817577ra/8056947.gif' width='400' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Book 1 - <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17828418.Fixed_on_You__Fixed___1_' title='Fixed on You (Fixed, #1) by Laurelin Paige' rel='nofollow noopener'>Fixed on You</a> </b>– Brilliant.<br/>Couldn’t put it down and didn’t want i</span>
  <span id="freeText15795938542373963434" style="display:none"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1390070552ra/8138415.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>**May Contain Spoilers**<br><br>Story Rating 4.5 Stars<br>Hero Rating 5 Stars <br>Heroine Rating 4 Stars<br>Romance Rating 4.5 Stars<br>Heat Level 5 Stars<br>Overall Rating 4.5 Stars</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1390070552ra/8138416.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I realized after I finished this book, that I haven’t written a review for ANY of the books in the series (not even as casting!), and I think the last one deserves a little something. <i>Not</i> that my reviews are literary masterpieces, but I did love this series, so...here goes.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389817577ra/8056947.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Book 1 - <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17828418.Fixed_on_You__Fixed___1_" title="Fixed on You (Fixed, #1) by Laurelin Paige" rel="nofollow noopener">Fixed on You</a> </b>– Brilliant.<br>Couldn’t put it down and didn’t want it to end.<br>It did remind me of the Crossfire Series by Sylvia Day, <i>but</i>, and I don’t say this lightly, it may be better. ONLY, in that I think Laurelin Paige did better in writing about the mental illness the characters had. It just seemed more believable to me. Don’t hate me<br><br><b>Book 2 - <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17930773.Found_in_You__Fixed___2_" title="Found in You (Fixed, #2) by Laurelin Paige" rel="nofollow noopener">Found in You</a></b> - Amazing!<br>Often times I’m let down by a books sequel. But this one, never!<br>This author, amazing!<br>Both books ended in a way that you knew there was more to the story, but you weren’t left with a cliffhanger, which is the worst. I think we can all agree, they are the absolute worst.<br>Writing in this book was again, spot on.<br>The characters developed even more.<br>The story got deeper.<br>You fell in love with Hudson all over again.<br>It was just MAGIC.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1390070552ra/8138417.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And, with all that, leads me to this book, the final book of the series.<br>And it was again, amazing.<br>We’re finally privy to all the dark secrets surrounding Hudson and Alayna, get to see them struggle to find a way to work through everything, and see them grow into better people because of it.<br>I will say though, the saving grace in each book (for me) has always been Hudson. He is one of the BEST better halves of an H/h pairing I’ve ever read.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1390070552ra/8138418.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>First, what I <i>didn’t</i> like…<br>While there are very few things I didn’t like about the book, that still leaves me with the fact there <i>were</i> things I didn’t like about the book.<br><b>One</b> – I did figure out the “twist” or secret. It ended up being somewhat predictable. Which is frustrating, because in the first two books, I had no idea. But for some reason, the writing in this book came apart a bit when it came to the big climax (no pun intended).<br><b>Two</b> - Alayna seemed to slip back into her old ways in this book. Which, kind of worked with how the story ended up going, but it was still annoying, made her seem to regress and less endearing…but that’s just my opinion.<br><b>Lastly</b> - Hudsons ability to say “I love you” was addressed. And, I didn’t care for how that worked out. Yes, <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[he finally said it. BUT, it never said why he had such an issue, and then when he finally did say it, it was like he never had an issue saying it before. His inability to say it before was never addressed, it was just smoothed over and forgotten. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. This, was dumb. I didn’t like it and it’s the only thing about Hudson’s character that annoyed me. Boo.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1390070552ra/8138419.gif" width="300" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>What I <i>did</i> like...<br><b>HUDSON</b><br>He’s so dreamy…le sigh.<br>He is what made each book of the series spectacular.<br>He was sexy.<br>He was endearing.<br>He was perfect.<br>Were his issues easy to love and perfect, no..but that’s what made <i>him</i> perfect, his flaws. That, and the way he was willing to change and be a better person for Alayna. <br>Gah, I just <b>love</b> him!<br>Besides Hudson, I’d have to say the writing and the authors ability to make the story unfold in a (mostly) seamless fashion, was extremely refreshing. I’ve basically given up on CR and NA books lately, because they’re all so similar and the writing seems rushed. This author and series, not so much. I could read these again and again and again…<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1390070552ra/8138420.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So, there you have it, the series was brilliant and so was this book.<br>I hope everyone who reads the series enjoys it as much as I did.<br>And, I can’t wait to read more about Gwen (spin off from this series) and anything else by Ms. Paige.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389982390ra/8119375.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Here’s my casting for Hudson (he's supposed to be more clean cut, but GAH, I love this guy!)…<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390070552i/8138421._SY540_.jpg" width="350" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

She's the meaning behind every one of my thoughts, every thrum of my pulse, every whisper of my conscience. She's my entire everything. It's as simple and as complex as that."</i>
</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/658533.gif" width="250" height="165" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>HOLY WOW I FEEL <b>WEEPY</b>. I just went through an <i>"anxiety inducing roller coaster of emotions"</i> ... Excuse me for the understatement.<br>The book was <i>heartbreaking</i> and <i>beautiful</i>, and everything in between. <br>It began just a couple hours after the last one left off. As it progresses, we find out that the same thing that had stood between them before, is still a giant obstacle on the road. That obstacle is <b>trust</b>. <br>This time, as they try to work their way closer to each other emotionally, <i>(since they have <b>so</b> got it down physically)</i>, it becomes clear that Hudson's trying to hide something <b>big</b>. And guys, by big, I mean <b>ENORMOUS</b><br><br>. . . <b>and so, you go through some fucked up shit</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1390179269ra/8158593.gif" width="356" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1390179269ra/8158596.gif" width="400" height="208" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Finally, you reach the end of the novel, and you can't help but shed some tears</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1390180754ra/8158914.gif" width="400" height="230" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>and you read the epilogue ... and swoon</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/680221.gif" width="400" height="218" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Then you finish reading the last words</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1390179269ra/8158597.gif" width="375" <i>AWESOMENESS</i></b> of the book, and really the entire series. <br>**Hint, hint** to the amazing author Laurelin Paige: <br><i>I'm really really hoping there's gonna be a novella of how it is a couple years later into their life; their future, their relationship, where they've gone...</i><br>Ultimately, the series was an unforgettable ride and I am <b>SO GLAD</b> to have given the first book, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17828418.Fixed_on_You__Fixed___1_" title="Fixed on You (Fixed, #1) by Laurelin Paige" rel="nofollow noopener">Fixed on You</a> a go. <br>Seriously, if you haven't read this, go get it. It's worth it.</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer822470590" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3481662654149932982">Laynie's insecurities became a bit much after awhile. She continuously made something out of nothing. I rolled my eyes so much I thought they'd get stuck in my head. To Hudson's credit he never did or said ANYTHING that should have caused such unwarranted reactions from Laynie. <br/><br/>Her compulsiveness began grating my nerves so badly that I would have to put the book down to regroup. I almost DNF. I get that she's broken and her way of thinking is obsessive but she just became so unlikable that being</span>
  <span id="freeText3481662654149932982" style="display:none">Laynie's insecurities became a bit much after awhile. She continuously made something out of nothing. I rolled my eyes so much I thought they'd get stuck in my head. To Hudson's credit he never did or said ANYTHING that should have caused such unwarranted reactions from Laynie. <br /><br />Her compulsiveness began grating my nerves so badly that I would have to put the book down to regroup. I almost DNF. I get that she's broken and her way of thinking is obsessive but she just became so unlikable that being in her head the entire time gave me a headache.<br /><br />My 3 star rating is all Hudson because had it not been for him I would have absolutely given up on this book. His patience towards Laynie and all her foolishness made him remarkable, granted the secret he kept hidden was a doozy but it was nothing compared to her behavior prior to it's big reveal. Had it been me in a relationship with Laynie I would have dropped her like a hot potato with a spider on it...<br /><br /><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="3481662654149932982" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('4MLDFz526lP60S7q9XEUwza6TKTk/e8a+25KWHariAx9/xZEl85HUfHXIcUNx6pc0PXffVvZe3pcdyXtO72ACw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {

    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }
